NV_BASIC#
Basic Skill
Max Level: 9
Skill Form: ^6666CCPassive^000000
Description: ^777777Enables the use of Basic
Interface Skills.^000000
[Lv 1]: Enables Trading
^777777You can trade ^990099Item^777777 and ^990099Zeny^777777 with other
^0033CCPlayer^777777.
^990000Right click on a player to initiate.^000000
[Lv 2]: Enables Emotions
^777777Alt+(0~9) and Ctrl+(1,-,=.)
Alt+L will open ^990099Emoticon Window^777777.^000000
[Lv 3]: Enables Sitting
^777777Doubles HP and SP regen speed.
^990000Press the Insert key or type /sit.^000000
[Lv 4]: Enables Chat Room Creation
^777777Alt+C to open a Chat Room.^000000
[Lv 5]: Joins a Party
^777777Character can join a party.^000000
[Lv 6]: Enables Use of Kafra Storage
^777777Talk to ^0033CCKafra Staff^777777 to open ^990099Storage^777777.^000000
[Lv 7]: Organize a Party
^777777Creates a party
Type ^990099/organize "Party Name"^777777
Set party options in the Party Window (Alt+Z).^000000
[Lv 9]: Enables Change to First Job Class
^777777Qualifies character for change from
^0033CCNovice^777777 to one of the ^0033CCFirst^777777 or ^0033CCExpanded^777777
classes.^000000
